***hoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> (297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hope</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hopa</i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hopon</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopen.html>hopen</a></i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hope</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hope, aspiration, wish</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopeloos.html>hopeloos</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoopgevend</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoopvol.html>hoopvol</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_4">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopen.html>hopen</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopen.html>hopen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hōp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haupaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopen.html>hopen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoopje.html>hoopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pile, heap, stack
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:berg.html>berg</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A lot, heaps</li>
<li>A pile of manure, <a href = vnd.unilang:faeces.html>faeces</a></li>
<li>A mass.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:massa.html>massa</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A multitude, a throng.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">drom</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:massa.html>massa</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:menigte.html>menigte</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schare.html>schare</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A unit of <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a>, a contingent.</li></ol>

***hoor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> (228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating reassurance or confidence from the speaker:</span> certainly, surely, at all, <span class="use-with-mention">but often weak and untranslatable</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straks.html>Straks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoeg.html>genoeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be late! — Nah, <b>surely</b> not, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> have plenty of time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>Wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonnetje.html>bonnetje</a>? — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bedankt.html>bedankt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you want the receipt? — No, <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating disagreement or a certain nuance with an earlier statement:</span> regardless, despite that, anyway, you know
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>kou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:valt.html>valt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a>. — <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cold isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> so bad. — Well, I still think it's pretty cold <b>regardless</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hoorn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a> (5582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*horn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hurną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">horn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Horn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hoarn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">horn</i>, Danish and Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">horn</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱer-</i>. Compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>, from the same origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoornen.html>hoornen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorns.html>hoorns</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorntje.html>hoorntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a horn (sound device) or a <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></li>
<li>a horn (growth projecting from the head of some animals)</li>
<li>a receiver, an earphone</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blazer.html>blazer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***hoorzitting.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorzitting.html>hoorzitting</a> (6389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitting.html>zitting</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">proceeding, meeting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in 1967.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hearing</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">proceeding for hearing arguments and discussion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1967</b> June 9, "Zenderpark Lopik <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> IJsselmeerpolders?", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>Waarheid</a></i>, issue 157, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Gedeputeerde <a href = vnd.unilang:staten.html>Staten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> week in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> zgn. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorzitting.html>hoorzitting</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partijen.html>partijen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluisterd.html>geluisterd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> 21 <a href = vnd.unilang:juni.html>juni</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standpunt.html>standpunt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Provincial Executive of <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> have listened in a so-called <b>hearing</b> to both parties this week and will determine their point of view on June 21.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***hoot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> (105292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:houten.html>houten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">huten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hoten</i>, of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span> origin, from or related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-osw">huta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cast out in contempt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">hiuzen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">hūzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to call to pursuit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">begone!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">interjection</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hui</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">huj</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoots</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A derisive cry or shout.</li>
<li>The cry of an owl.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fun event or person. (See hootenanny)</li>
<li>A small particle.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1878</b>,  John Hanson Beadle,  <cite>Western <a href = vnd.unilang:wilds.html>Wilds</a>, and the <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a> who Redeem Them</cite>, Jones Brothers, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/7349592">7349592</a></small>, page 611:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Well, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Sunday morning, and the wheat nothing like ripe; but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a chance, and I got onto my <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a> and banged down every <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> of it before Monday night.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">small particle</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nearly always encountered in a negative sense in such phrases as <i>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> care a <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></i> or <i>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> give two hoots</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derisive cry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The phrase <i>a <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> and a <a href = vnd.unilang:holler.html>holler</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a very different meaning to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:holler.html>holler</a></i>. The former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a short distance, the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a verb of <i>derisive cry</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hoots</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hooting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hooted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To cry out or shout in contempt.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1711</b>,  John Dryden,  “Satire IX”, in  <cite>Dryden’s <a href = vnd.unilang:juvenal.html>Juvenal</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Matrons and <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a> shall <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> at <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> no more,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To make the cry of an owl.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1595–1596</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Midsummer_Night%27s_Dream" class="extiw" title="w:A Midsummer Night | s Dream">A Midsommer <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> Dreame</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>,  | Act II, scene ii | :</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The clamorous owl that nightly <b>hoots</b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wonders.html>wonders</a> / At our quaint <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To assail with contemptuous cries or shouts; to follow with derisive shouts.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1708</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Bickerstaff" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Isaac Bickerstaff">Isaac Bickerstaff</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> Swift],  <cite>Predictions for the Year 1708</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://jonathanswiftarchive.org.uk/search/text_4_3_2.html?page=d2e215">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And I will be content, that Partridge, and the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of his Clan, may <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> for a Cheat and Impostor, if I fail in any single Particular of <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>Moment</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To sound the horn of a vehicle</li></ol>
</body>

***hopper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a> (6616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hoppere</i>, alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*hoppe</i> (found in <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gras-hoppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoppa.html>hoppa</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who hops, <a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hop</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hoppare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a>, jumper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">hoppari</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoppers</b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG/160px-Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG" decoding="async" width="160" height="152" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG/240px-Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG/320px-Tolva_de_inyeccion_de_extrusion_de_polimeros.JPG 2x" data-file-width="947" data-file-height="897" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></b> (funnel-shaped bin)</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Detail_of_hopper_windows_at_bathroom._-_Naval_Supply_Annex_Stockton%2C_Pass_Office%2C_North_of_Main_Gate_on_Fyffe_Avenue%2C_Stockton%2C_San_Joaquin_County%2C_CA_HABS_CAL%2C39-STOCK%2C33B-7.tif/lossy-page1-160px-thumbnail.tif.jpg" decoding="async" width="160" height="200" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Detail_of_hopper_windows_at_bathroom._-_Naval_Supply_Annex_Stockton%2C_Pass_Office%2C_North_of_Main_Gate_on_Fyffe_Avenue%2C_Stockton%2C_San_Joaquin_County%2C_CA_HABS_CAL%2C39-STOCK%2C33B-7.tif/lossy-page1-240px-thumbnail.tif.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Detail_of_hopper_windows_at_bathroom._-_Naval_Supply_Annex_Stockton%2C_Pass_Office%2C_North_of_Main_Gate_on_Fyffe_Avenue%2C_Stockton%2C_San_Joaquin_County%2C_CA_HABS_CAL%2C39-STOCK%2C33B-7.tif/lossy-page1-320px-thumbnail.tif.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3999" data-file-height="5000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></b> window</div></div></div>
<ol><li>One who or that which hops.</li>
<li>A temporary storage bin, filled from the top and emptied from the bottom, often funnel-shaped.</li>
<li>A funnel-shaped section at the top of a drainpipe used to collect water, from above, from one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> drainpipes.</li>
<li>A device that feeds material into a machine.</li>
<li>Various insects
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> or locust, especially:
<ol><li>The immature form of a locust.</li></ol></li>
<li>The larva of a cheese fly.</li>
<li>A leafhopper.</li>
<li>Any of various hesperiid butterflies.</li></ol></li>
<li>An artificial fishing lure.
<dl><dd><i>To catch a big fish, use a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></b> that jumps across the <a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a> surface.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Robert Hudson, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a> of an Unusual Life</i> (page 250)
<dl><dd>The fresh-water container for the house <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> above the ceiling directly <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>. One day, I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> comfortably seated on the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></b> minding my own business, when a large portion of the ceiling <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> crashing down <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An escapement <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> in a <a href = vnd.unilang:piano.html>piano</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The game of hopscotch.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Johnson to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A window with hinges at the bottom, opened by tilting vertically.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a> car.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fairy chess piece which <a href = vnd.unilang:moves.html>moves</a> only by <a href = vnd.unilang:jumping.html>jumping</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> another piece.</li>
<li>A person or machine that picks hops.</li></ol>

***horen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a> (304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hōren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hauʀijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauzijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ḱh₂owsyéti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>hear</b> nothing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to belong
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>belong</b> with us.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be supposed to, to be meant to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> supposed to</b> be lying here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be appropriate, polite or agreeing with social <a href = vnd.unilang:norms.html>norms</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. to be <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> of)

***horloge.html

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orlogie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">orloge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hōrologium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὡρολόγιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hōrológion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***hormoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hormoon.html>hormoon</a> (30507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hormoon.html>hormoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hormonen.html>hormonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hormoon.html>hormoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hormone (substance produced by the body that physiologically affects bodily activity)</li></ol>

***horny.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a> (51683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">horn</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hornig</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hoornachtig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hornaktig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hyrniġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">angular</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">hornier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">horniest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Hard or bony, like an animal's horn.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">callous</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">coarse</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hardened</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rough</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1951</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C._S._Lewis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:C. S. Lewis">C. S. <a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prince_Caspian" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Prince Caspian">Prince Caspian</a></i>, Collins, 1998, Chapter 6,
<dl><dd>Two Dwarfs <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> at the <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a>, another <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> holding a piece of red-hot metal on the anvil with a pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a>, a fourth <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hammering it, and two, wiping their <b><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></b> little hands on a greasy cloth, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> coming forward to meet the visitors.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Having horns.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">horned</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:karen.html>Karen</a> M. Dvornich,  “Short-horned Lizard”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20101028054955/http://depts.washington.edu/natmap/projects/waterville/begin.html">[1]</a></sup>, archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://depts.washington.edu/natmap/projects/waterville/begin.html">the original</a> on <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2010-10-28">2010-10-28</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In 1997, 4th and 5th grade Waterville Elementary students <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> they saw Short-horned <a href = vnd.unilang:lizards.html>lizards</a> (commonly known as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>Horny</a></b> toads) all around their area.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sexually aroused.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">toey</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">in heat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">excited</span>; <i>see also</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That girl <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> feel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1949</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Miller" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Miller"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Miller</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sexus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sexus">Sexus</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Her thick, gurgling voice saying...: "Get it in all the way... please, please do... <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1971</b> October,  <cite>Black World</cite>, page 65/1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Ain’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> that the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> grindin with the <a href = vnd.unilang:blind.html>blind</a> dude.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sexy.html>sexy</a></span></span></dd></dl>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>hors</a> (27119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hursa-</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>hors</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>horsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>horsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now mostly found in names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">horse</span>
<ul><li><b>1558</b>, Gaathije Pietersz, "<a href = vnd.unilang:inventaris.html>Inventaris</a>, gemaeckt den IV<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></small></small> Januarii <a href = vnd.unilang:anno.html>anno</a> XV<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em">C</small></small> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> ende vijftich", in <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> Hallema, "<a href = vnd.unilang:nogmaals.html>Nogmaals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drietal.html>drietal</a> inventarissen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Franeker <a href = vnd.unilang:burgers.html>burgers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kort.html>kort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> 1550", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijdragen.html>Bijdragen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Mededeelingen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>Historisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genootschap.html>Genootschap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 49, 1928, 286.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> coopbrief ende quitantie, gepasseert by Fopke Wopkezn. ende Hessel Thomaszn., <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> mombers <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Pieterszoons weesen, aen Jan Jacobszn. ende <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> Jans <a href = vnd.unilang:dochter.html>dochter</a>, vanden huijsinge <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> Syaerda, mit hecken, heckpalen, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftien.html>vijftien</a> koeijen, <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> rieren, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> os, <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>horsen</a></b> ende <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dieren.html>dieren</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> gecoft ende betaelt <a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> hundert ende <a href = vnd.unilang:anderhalf.html>anderhalf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gouden.html>gouden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:guldens.html>guldens</a>, sijnde in date den XXI<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></small></small> Novembris <a href = vnd.unilang:anno.html>anno</a> 1549;</dd></dl></li>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetbaar.html>eetbare</a> vissoort <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Trachurus_trachurus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Trachurus trachurus"><span style="color:green;"><i>Trachurus trachurus</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorkomt.html>voorkomt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oostelijke.html>oostelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:atlantische.html>Atlantische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oceaan.html>Oceaan</a></li></ol>

<ul><li>horsmakreel</li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord_2"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>hors</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>

<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>horst</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>Horst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>horst</a>; eyrie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an area of the earth's surface which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> raised relative to surrounding <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>; a <a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>horst</a></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hôtel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">hostel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ostel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hospitālis</i>. ***houden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> (232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">haldan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haldaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a particular state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tanden.html>tanden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You should <b>keep</b> your teeth properly clean.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***housewarming.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:housewarming.html>housewarming</a> (60659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">house</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">warming</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:housewarming.html>housewarming</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">housewarmings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A party to celebrate moving into a new home.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 5, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Farquhar Fenelon Cooke the apotheosis of the Celebrity <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> complete. The people of Asquith <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not only willing to attend the <b>house-warming</b>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> worked up to the pitch of eagerness.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>The act of welcoming a person/family to their newly purchased or newly rented home.
<dl><dd><i>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:housewarming.html>housewarming</a></b> gift</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> M <a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>Appel</a>,  “Gadney's Immunity”, in  <cite>Southwest Review</cite>, volume 89, number 4, page 580:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">They <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> their first argument on the evening Gadney moved in, their <b><a href = vnd.unilang:housewarming.html>housewarming</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:spat.html>spat</a>, he <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> called it.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hout.html>hout</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">holt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hultą</i>.

***houvast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:houvast.html>houvast</a> (15811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houd.html>houd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></i>, the imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vasthouden.html>vasthouden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold tight onto</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">holdfast</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houvast.html>houvast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a>, grasp</li>
<li>something to hold onto <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">physically or emotionally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, support, solace</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">court, yard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ier</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovenier.html>hovenier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovenier.html>hoveniers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovenier.html>hoveniertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Professional gardener</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used for a gardener that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> contracted. A gardener who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> permanently employed by the owner of the garden <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more likely to be called a "<a href = vnd.unilang:tuinman.html>tuinman</a>".
</p>

***hovercraft.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hovercraft.html>hovercraft</a> (49322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hover</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-craft</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovercraft.html>hovercraft</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovercrafts.html>hovercrafts</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:hovercraft.html>hovercraft</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A vehicle supported on a cushion of air, able to traverse many different <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of terrain and travel <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> water, used for transport.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ACV</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">air-cushion vehicle</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">GEM</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ground-effect machine</span></li></ul>
